**Version:** 1.0
**Date:** January 2, 2026

**Target:** Small-to-mid construction contractors

## 1. Executive Summary

### What is SiteLink?

SiteLink is a mobile-first construction plan viewer that automatically detects and links callout symbols between sheets, enabling one-tap navigation. It combines plan viewing with photo documentation, allowing field workers to capture and organize work photos by plan reference.

### Core Value Proposition

1. **Auto-linking that works** - 91.5% recall on callout detection, no manual hyperlinking
2. **Photo-first documentation** - Timeline-based photo capture, not task management
3. **Radical simplicity** - 5 features vs competitors' 50+
4. **Aggressive pricing** - $79/month flat vs $195+/month for comparable features
5. **True offline-first** - LiveStore event sourcing for reliable field operation

### Technical Foundation

Built on **LiveStore** (local-first, event-sourcing data layer) for:

- Full offline operation with automatic sync
- Built-in audit trail ("who did what when")
- Reactive queries for instant UI updates
- Conflict-free sync across devices

### What SiteLink is NOT

- Task management system (photos ARE the documentation)
- RFI/submittal workflow tool
- Budget/cost tracker
- Enterprise compliance platform
- BIM viewer

---

## 2. Market Position & Differentiation

### Competitive Landscape

| Product        | Price (5 users) | Auto-Linking    | Complexity | Target                |
| -------------- | --------------- | --------------- | ---------- | --------------------- |
| Fieldwire      | $195/mo         | Yes             | Medium     | Mid-size GCs          |
| Autodesk Build | $675/mo         | Yes             | High       | Enterprise            |
| Procore        | $375+/mo        | Yes             | Very High  | Enterprise            |
| **SiteLink**   | **$79/mo**      | **Yes (91.5%)** | **Low**    | **Small contractors** |

### Differentiation Strategy

| Competitor Weakness              | SiteLink Advantage                |
| -------------------------------- | --------------------------------- |
| Complex setup (30+ min)          | 60-second setup                   |
| Per-user pricing adds up         | Flat monthly pricing              |
| Features field workers never use | Only what matters                 |
| Enterprise-focused               | Small contractor focused          |
| Requires training                | Self-explanatory                  |
| Partial offline support          | True offline-first (LiveStore)    |
| No audit trail                   | Event sourcing = built-in history |

### Target Customer

- 1-20 person construction companies
- Residential and small commercial
- Electricians, plumbers, HVAC, general contractors
- Currently using: Paper plans, basic PDF viewers, or nothing

---

## 3. User Personas

### Primary: Field Worker ("Mike the Electrician")

```
Name: Mike
Role: Journeyman Electrician
Age: 38
Tech comfort: Medium (uses smartphone daily, not apps for work)
Pain points:
- Scrolling through 50+ PDF sheets to find a detail
- Can't type with work gloves on
- No cell service in some areas
- Hates "another app to learn"

Needs:
- Find the right sheet fast
- Take photos to document work
- Share with boss/inspector
- Works offline

Quote: "I just need to see the plans and take some pictures.
       I don't need all that other stuff."
```

### Secondary: Small Business Owner ("Sarah the GC")

```
Name: Sarah
Role: General Contractor, owns 8-person company
Age: 45
Tech comfort: Medium-high
Pain points:
- Workers don't update task systems
- Spends time on daily reports
- Can't justify $200+/month on software
- Hard to get subs to use another app

Needs:
- Know what work was done each day
- Share plans with subcontractors easily
- Professional reports for clients
- Affordable pricing

Quote: "I've tried Fieldwire and Procore. My guys just
       won't use them. Too complicated."
```

### Tertiary: Subcontractor ("Carlos the Plumber")

```
Name: Carlos
Role: Plumbing subcontractor, 3-person crew
Age: 52
Tech comfort: Low-medium
Pain points:
- GC uses different software on every job
- Doesn't want to pay for software
- Just needs to see what to do
- Needs to send photos to inspector

Needs:
- View plans GC shares with him (free)
- Take photos for his records
- Simple, no learning curve

Quote: "Just send me the plans. I don't want to
       create another account."
```

### Navigation Patterns

| Pattern              | When Used                    | Example                       |
| -------------------- | ---------------------------- | ----------------------------- |
| Tab switch           | Moving between main sections | Plans â†’ Camera                |
| Push (stack)         | Drilling into detail         | Project List â†’ Project Detail |
| Modal (bottom sheet) | Quick actions                | Callout tap â†’ Action Sheet    |
| Full-screen modal    | Focused tasks                | Photo capture, Checkout       |
| Overlay              | Non-blocking info            | Toast notifications           |

```
â”‚   â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜   â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚         This usually takes 1-3 minutes.                    â”‚
â”‚       You can close this and we'll notify you.             â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                             â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Processing Steps:
1. Splitting PDF pages (fast, ~5 seconds)
2. Generating high-res tiles (slow, ~30 sec/page)
3. Extracting sheet metadata via OCR (medium, ~10 sec/page)
4. Detecting callout markers (medium, ~5 sec/page)

Behavior:
- User can navigate away; processing continues
- Push notification when complete
- If user stays, auto-navigates to Plans tab when done
```

```
- Photos taken offline are queued for upload when online
- "Update" re-downloads latest version
- "âœ•" removes download (confirmation dialog)
```

```
Behavior:
- Submit creates feature request in backlog (internal tool)
- Popular requests sorted by vote count
- User can upvote existing requests
- Logged-in users can only vote once per request
```

---

## 8. AI Features Specification

### 8.1 Voice Notes with Transcription

**Trigger:** User taps "Add Voice" after taking photo

**Input:**

- Audio file (m4a/webm, max 60 seconds)
- Associated photo ID
- Associated callout ID (if linked)

**Processing:**

1. Audio uploaded to R2 storage
2. Whisper API called asynchronously
3. Transcription stored in database

**Output:**

- Original audio (playable)
- Transcription text (searchable)

**API:** OpenAI Whisper or Cloudflare Workers AI
**Cost:** ~$0.006/minute of audio
**Latency:** 2-5 seconds for 30-second clip

**UI States:**

```
Recording:     "ğŸ”´ Recording... 0:03"
Uploading:     "Saving voice note..."
Transcribing:  "ğŸ¤ Voice note (0:05) â³ Transcribing..."
Complete:      "ğŸ¤ Voice note (0:05) â–¶ï¸"
               "Junction box needs to move..."
Error:         "ğŸ¤ Voice note (0:05) â–¶ï¸"
               "âš ï¸ Transcription failed [Retry]"
```

### 8.2 Plan Text Search

**Trigger:** User taps search icon in Plans tab, types query

**Processing:**

1. During plan upload: OCR all sheets, store text with bounding boxes
2. Build full-text search index (PostgreSQL FTS or Typesense)
3. On search: Query index, return matches with snippets

**Input:**

- Search query string
- Current project ID

**Output:**

- List of sheets containing matches
- Match count per sheet
- Snippet with match highlighted

**Storage:** ~10KB text per sheet average
**Search latency:** <200ms

### 8.3 Photo Text Extraction (OCR)

**Trigger:** Automatic on photo capture (background)

**Processing:**

1. Photo uploaded
2. PaddleOCR extracts text
3. Text stored with photo metadata

**Output:**

- Extracted text (editable by user)
- Searchable in photo search

**Display:** Only shown if text detected (>10 characters)
**Cost:** Negligible (already running PaddleOCR)

### 8.4 Daily Summary Generation

**Trigger:** User taps "Generate Daily Summary" in Project Detail

**Input:**

- All photos from selected date
- All voice note transcriptions
- Issue flags
- Callout references
- Project metadata (name, address)
- Weather data (from address, optional)

**Prompt Template:**

```
Generate a professional Daily Construction Report from the following data:

Project: {project_name}
Address: {address}
Date: {date}
Weather: {weather}

Photos captured today:
{for each photo}
- Time: {timestamp}
- Location: {callout_reference or "General"}
- Issue: {yes/no}
- Voice note: "{transcription}"
{end for}

Format the report with these sections:
1. WORK PERFORMED - summarize what was done based on callout locations
2. ISSUES / DELAYS - list any flagged issues with quotes from voice notes
3. MATERIALS RECEIVED - if mentioned in voice notes, otherwise "None noted"
4. PHOTOS - mention total count

Keep it professional and concise. Use construction industry terminology.
```

**Model:** Gemini 2.0 Flash (fast, cheap) or Claude 3.5 Haiku
**Cost:** ~$0.01-0.02 per summary
**Latency:** 3-8 seconds

### 8.5 RFI Draft Generation

**Trigger:** User taps "Generate RFI" on issue photo

**Input:**

- Issue photo
- Voice note transcription
- Callout reference (sheet number, detail number)
- Project metadata

**Prompt Template:**

```
Generate a professional Request for Information (RFI) draft for construction:

Project: {project_name}
Reference: Detail {callout_id} on Sheet {sheet_number}
Issue Description (from field): "{voice_transcription}"

The RFI should:
1. Clearly describe the field condition discovered
2. Reference the specific drawing detail
3. Ask a specific question requiring architect/engineer response
4. Maintain professional tone

Format:
To: [Architect/Engineer]
Re: {brief subject line}

Description:
{2-3 sentences describing the issue}

Request:
{specific question}

Attachments referenced: Photo dated {date}
```

**Model:** Claude 3.5 Sonnet (quality matters for professional docs)
**Cost:** ~$0.02-0.05 per RFI
**Latency:** 5-10 seconds

---

## 9. Offline Mode

### 9.1 What Works Offline

| Feature                | Offline Support    | Notes                                    |
| ---------------------- | ------------------ | ---------------------------------------- |
| View downloaded plans  | âœ… Full            | Tiles stored locally                     |
| Pan/zoom plans         | âœ… Full            |                                          |
| Tap callout markers    | âœ… Full            | Links work within downloaded sheets      |
| Take photos            | âœ… Full            | Stored locally, queued for upload        |
| Record voice notes     | âœ… Full            | Stored locally, queued for transcription |
| View existing photos   | âœ… Downloaded only | Only photos included in download         |
| Search plans           | âŒ No              | Requires server                          |
| Generate daily summary | âŒ No              | Requires LLM API                         |
| Upload new plans       | âŒ No              | Requires server processing               |
| Share project          | âŒ No              | Requires server                          |

### 9.3 Offline Sync (LiveStore)

LiveStore handles offline sync automatically via event sourcing:

```
HOW IT WORKS:

1. User captures photo offline
   â””â”€â–¶ photoCaptured event committed locally
   â””â”€â–¶ State updated immediately (UI shows photo)
   â””â”€â–¶ Event queued in local eventlog

2. Device comes back online
   â””â”€â–¶ LiveStore pushes queued events to sync backend
   â””â”€â–¶ Photo file uploaded to R2 separately
   â””â”€â–¶ photoUploaded event committed when complete

3. Other devices
   â””â”€â–¶ Pull events from sync backend
   â””â”€â–¶ Materializers replay events â†’ state updated
   â””â”€â–¶ UI updates reactively
```

```
SYNC STATUS UI:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Syncing...                                          [âœ•]   â”‚
â”‚  â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€  â”‚
â”‚  Uploading 5 photos taken offline                          â”‚
â”‚  â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘  3 of 5                             â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Sync priority:
1. Events (lightweight, instant)
2. Photos (larger files)
3. Voice notes (audio files)

If sync fails:
- LiveStore retries automatically
- Events are never lost (persisted locally)
- User can force retry from settings
```

### 9.4 Offline Indicator

```
WHEN OFFLINE, SHOW IN HEADER:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

Tapping shows: "You're offline. Some features unavailable."
```

---

## 10. Notifications

### 10.1 Push Notification Types

| Notification             | Trigger                      | Content                                                     |
| ------------------------ | ---------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------- |
| Plan processing complete | Plans finished processing    | "Your plans are ready! 47 sheets processed."                |
| Issue flagged            | Team member flags issue      | "Mike flagged an issue at 5/A7"                             |
| Team activity            | Photos added by others       | "Sarah added 5 photos to Riverside Apartments"              |
| Daily summary reminder   | 5 PM local time (if enabled) | "Ready to generate today's summary? 12 photos captured."    |
| Trial ending             | 3 days before trial ends     | "Your trial ends in 3 days. Upgrade to keep your projects." |
| Trial expired            | Day trial ends               | "Your trial has ended. Upgrade to continue editing."        |
| Subscription renewed     | Monthly renewal              | "Your Pro subscription renewed. Thanks for using SiteLink!" |
| Subscription failed      | Payment failed               | "Payment failed. Update your card to keep Pro features."    |

### 10.2 In-App Notification Center

```
NOT IMPLEMENTED IN MVP

Future consideration: Bell icon in header showing notification history
For MVP: Push notifications only, no in-app notification center
```

### 10.3 Notification Deep Links

| Notification             | Deep Link Target                  |
| ------------------------ | --------------------------------- |
| Plan processing complete | Plans Tab (project auto-selected) |
| Issue flagged            | Photo Timeline for that callout   |
| Team activity            | Project Detail                    |
| Daily summary reminder   | Project Detail                    |
| Trial ending/expired     | Subscription screen               |
| Subscription issues      | Subscription screen               |

## 11. Payment & Subscription

### 11.1 Pricing Tiers

| Tier         | Price   | Projects  | Users     | Sheets    | Features                     |
| ------------ | ------- | --------- | --------- | --------- | ---------------------------- |
| **Starter**  | $29/mo  | 1         | 3         | 500       | Core (no AI)                 |
| **Pro**      | $79/mo  | 5         | 15        | Unlimited | + Voice, Search, Summaries   |
| **Business** | $149/mo | Unlimited | Unlimited | Unlimited | + RFI, API, Priority Support |

### 11.2 Feature Availability by Tier

| Feature                        | Starter | Pro | Business |
| ------------------------------ | ------- | --- | -------- |
| Plan viewing + callout linking | âœ…      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Photo capture + timeline       | âœ…      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Voice notes (audio only)       | âœ…      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Share view-only links          | âœ…      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Offline downloads              | âœ…      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Voice transcription            | âŒ      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Plan text search               | âŒ      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Photo text extraction (OCR)    | âŒ      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| Daily summary generation       | âŒ      | âœ…  | âœ…       |
| RFI draft generation           | âŒ      | âŒ  | âœ…       |
| API access                     | âŒ      | âŒ  | âœ…       |
| Priority support               | âŒ      | âŒ  | âœ…       |
| Custom report branding         | âŒ      | âŒ  | âœ…       |

### 11.3 Trial Details

- **Duration:** 14 days
- **Features:** Full Pro access
- **Credit card:** Not required to start
- **Limits:** Same as Pro tier
- **At expiration:** Projects become read-only (not deleted)
- **Grace period:** 30 days before data deletion warning

### 11.4 Polar Integration

**Setup:**

```typescript
// backend/src/auth/index.ts
import { polar, checkout, portal } from "@polar-sh/better-auth"

const auth = betterAuth({
  plugins: [
    polar({
      client: polarClient,
      createCustomerOnSignUp: true,
      use: [
        checkout({
          products: [
            { productId: STARTER_PRODUCT_ID, slug: "starter" },
            { productId: PRO_PRODUCT_ID, slug: "pro" },
            { productId: BUSINESS_PRODUCT_ID, slug: "business" },
          ],
          successUrl: "/subscription/success",
        }),
        portal(),
      ],
    }),
  ],
})
```

**Checkout Flow:**

1. User taps "Select" on plan
2. App calls `authClient.checkout({ slug: "pro" })`
3. Polar embedded checkout opens as overlay
4. User enters payment details
5. Polar handles payment processing
6. Webhook received: `subscription.created`
7. App updates user's subscription status
8. Success screen shown

**Subscription Management:**

- "Manage Subscription" opens Polar Customer Portal
- User can update payment method, cancel, view invoices
- Cancellation effective at end of billing period

---

## 12. Analytics & Tracking

### 12.1 Events to Track

**Onboarding:**
| Event | Properties | Purpose |
|-------|------------|---------|
| `app_opened` | `first_open: boolean` | Measure installs |
| `signup_started` | `method: google/microsoft/email` | Conversion funnel |
| `signup_completed` | `method, trial_started: boolean` | Conversion funnel |
| `first_project_created` | `time_since_signup` | Activation |
| `first_plans_uploaded` | `sheet_count, time_since_signup` | Activation |
| `plans_processing_complete` | `sheet_count, duration_seconds` | Performance |

**Core Usage:**
| Event | Properties | Purpose |
|-------|------------|---------|
| `sheet_viewed` | `sheet_id, project_id, duration_seconds` | Engagement |
| `callout_tapped` | `callout_id, navigated: boolean` | Feature usage |
| `photo_captured` | `linked_to_callout: boolean, is_issue: boolean` | Core workflow |
| `voice_note_recorded` | `duration_seconds, callout_id` | Feature usage |
| `search_performed` | `query_length, result_count` | Feature usage |
| `daily_summary_generated` | `photo_count, issue_count` | AI usage |
| `rfi_draft_generated` | `callout_id` | AI usage |

**Sharing:**
| Event | Properties | Purpose |
|-------|------------|---------|
| `share_link_created` | `type: project/report, project_id` | Virality |
| `share_link_viewed` | `link_id, viewer_signed_up: boolean` | Virality |
| `team_member_invited` | `project_id, method: link/email` | Growth |

**Subscription:**
| Event | Properties | Purpose |
|-------|------------|---------|
| `upgrade_prompt_shown` | `trigger: trial_ending/limit_hit/manual` | Conversion |
| `checkout_started` | `plan: starter/pro/business` | Conversion |
| `subscription_created` | `plan, trial_converted: boolean` | Revenue |
| `subscription_cancelled` | `plan, reason: string (optional)` | Churn |

**Errors:**
| Event | Properties | Purpose |
|-------|------------|---------|
| `error_occurred` | `type, message, screen` | Debugging |
| `upload_failed` | `file_size, error_type` | Reliability |
| `sync_failed` | `item_type, error_type` | Offline reliability |

### 12.2 Analytics Dashboard Metrics

**For internal monitoring:**

| Metric             | Definition                               | Target  |
| ------------------ | ---------------------------------------- | ------- |
| DAU                | Daily active users                       | Growing |
| WAU                | Weekly active users                      | Growing |
| Activation rate    | % signups who upload plans within 7 days | >60%    |
| Photo capture rate | Avg photos per active user per day       | >5      |
| Trial conversion   | % trials that convert to paid            | >15%    |
| Churn rate         | Monthly % paid users who cancel          | <5%     |
| NPS                | Net Promoter Score (from in-app survey)  | >50     |

### 12.3 User-Facing Reports (Future)

**Project Activity Report (Business tier):**

- Photos captured per day/week/month
- Team member activity breakdown
- Issues flagged and resolved
- Most active callouts/areas

---

## 13. Share & Collaboration

### 13.1 Share Types

| Share Type          | Who Can View     | Auth Required          | Expires                |
| ------------------- | ---------------- | ---------------------- | ---------------------- |
| Project (view-only) | Anyone with link | No                     | Never (until revoked)  |
| Daily Report        | Anyone with link | No                     | 30 days (configurable) |
| Full Project Access | Invited members  | Yes (account required) | Never                  |

### 13.2 View-Only Project Share

**What shared users can do:**

- View all plan sheets
- Navigate via callout links
- View photos (but not add)
- Download sheets for offline

**What shared users cannot do:**

- Add photos
- Record voice notes
- Generate summaries
- Invite others
- Modify project

### 13.3 Team Member Roles

| Role       | Permissions                                 |
| ---------- | ------------------------------------------- |
| **Owner**  | Full access, billing, can delete project    |
| **Admin**  | Full access except billing                  |
| **Member** | View plans, add photos, generate summaries  |
| **Viewer** | View only (same as share link, but tracked) |

## 14. Feedback & Feature Requests

### 14.1 In-App Feedback Points

| Location      | Type            | Trigger                            |
| ------------- | --------------- | ---------------------------------- |
| More Tab      | Feature Request | Manual tap                         |
| Photo capture | Quick feedback  | After 10th photo (first time only) |
| Daily summary | Quality rating  | After viewing summary              |
| Support chat  | Bug report      | Manual tap                         |
| Trial ending  | Exit survey     | When not converting                |

### 14.3 Feature Request Tracking

**Stored fields:**

- User ID
- Request text
- Category
- Timestamp
- Upvote count
- Status (new/planned/in-progress/shipped/declined)

**Internal review:**

- Weekly review of new requests
- Top-voted requests prioritized in roadmap
- Users notified when their request ships

## 15. Design System

### 15.1 Colors

```
PRIMARY
- Blue-600:    #2563EB (Primary actions, links)
- Blue-700:    #1D4ED8 (Pressed state)
- Blue-100:    #DBEAFE (Backgrounds, highlights)

SEMANTIC
- Red-500:     #EF4444 (Issues, errors, destructive)
- Red-100:     #FEE2E2 (Issue backgrounds)
- Green-500:   #22C55E (Success, complete)
- Yellow-500:  #F59E0B (Warnings)

NEUTRAL
- Gray-900:    #111827 (Primary text)
- Gray-700:    #374151 (Secondary text)
- Gray-500:    #6B7280 (Tertiary text, icons)
- Gray-300:    #D1D5DB (Borders)
- Gray-100:    #F3F4F6 (Backgrounds)
- White:       #FFFFFF (Cards, surfaces)

DISCIPLINE BADGES
- ARCH:        #3B82F6 (Blue)
- ELEC:        #F59E0B (Amber)
- STRC:        #8B5CF6 (Purple)
- MECH:        #10B981 (Emerald)
- PLMB:        #06B6D4 (Cyan)
- SITE:        #84CC16 (Lime)
```

### 15.2 Typography

```
FONT FAMILY
- iOS: SF Pro (system)
- Android: Roboto (system)

SIZES
- Heading 1:   28pt / 34pt line height (Bold)
- Heading 2:   22pt / 28pt line height (Semi-bold)
- Heading 3:   18pt / 24pt line height (Semi-bold)
- Body:        16pt / 24pt line height (Regular)
- Body Small:  14pt / 20pt line height (Regular)
- Caption:     12pt / 16pt line height (Regular)
- Label:       10pt / 12pt line height (Medium, uppercase)
```

### 15.3 Spacing

```
BASE UNIT: 4pt

- XS:  4pt   (tight spacing within components)
- S:   8pt   (between related elements)
- M:   16pt  (between sections)
- L:   24pt  (major sections, screen padding)
- XL:  32pt  (hero spacing)
- XXL: 48pt  (page-level separation)

SCREEN PADDING: 16pt horizontal
CARD PADDING: 16pt all sides
LIST ITEM HEIGHT: 56pt minimum (touch target)
```

### 15.4 Components

**Buttons:**

```
PRIMARY BUTTON
- Height: 56pt
- Radius: 12pt
- Background: Blue-600
- Text: White, 16pt Semi-bold
- Pressed: Blue-700

SECONDARY BUTTON
- Height: 56pt
- Radius: 12pt
- Background: White
- Border: 1pt Gray-300
- Text: Gray-900, 16pt Medium
- Pressed: Gray-100 background

TEXT BUTTON
- Height: 44pt
- Text: Blue-600, 16pt Medium
- Pressed: Blue-700

DESTRUCTIVE BUTTON
- Same as Primary but Red-500/Red-600
```

**Input Fields:**

```
TEXT INPUT
- Height: 52pt
- Radius: 8pt
- Border: 1pt Gray-300
- Focus border: 2pt Blue-600
- Padding: 16pt horizontal
- Text: 16pt Gray-900
- Placeholder: 16pt Gray-500
```

**Cards:**

```
CARD
- Background: White
- Radius: 12pt
- Shadow: 0 1pt 3pt rgba(0,0,0,0.1)
- Padding: 16pt
```

### 15.5 Touch Targets

```
MINIMUM TOUCH TARGET: 44pt Ã— 44pt (Apple HIG)

For construction/gloved use, prefer:
- Buttons: 56pt height minimum
- List items: 56pt height minimum
- Icon buttons: 48pt Ã— 48pt minimum
- Shutter button: 72pt diameter
```

---

## 16. Technical Considerations

### 16.1 Tech Stack

| Layer              | Technology                                                    |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Mobile App         | Expo (React Native)                                           |
| State Management   | LiveStore (local-first, event sourcing)                       |
| Local Storage      | expo-sqlite (via LiveStore adapter)                           |
| Sync Backend       | Cloudflare Workers + Durable Objects (via @livestore/sync-cf) |
| Plan Viewer        | OpenSeadragon (via DOM Components)                            |
| Backend API        | Cloudflare Workers + Effect-TS                                |
| File Storage       | Cloudflare R2                                                 |
| Auth               | Better-Auth                                                   |
| Payments           | Polar                                                         |
| OCR                | PaddleOCR (Docker container)                                  |
| Tile Generation    | vips (Docker container)                                       |
| AI - Transcription | Whisper (OpenAI or CF Workers AI)                             |
| AI - Summaries     | Gemini 2.0 Flash                                              |
| AI - RFI           | Claude 3.5 Sonnet                                             |
| Analytics          | PostHog                                                       |

### 16.1.1 Why LiveStore?

LiveStore is a local-first data layer using event sourcing. Benefits for SiteLink:

| Benefit                 | How It Helps                                                    |
| ----------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Offline-first**       | Field workers have poor connectivity; works fully offline       |
| **Event sourcing**      | Built-in audit trail: "who did what when" for construction docs |
| **Reactive queries**    | UI updates instantly when data changes                          |
| **Automatic sync**      | Events queue locally, sync when online - no manual sync code    |
| **Conflict resolution** | Handles concurrent edits from multiple devices                  |

### 16.2 Data Models (LiveStore)

SiteLink uses LiveStore's event sourcing pattern. State (SQLite tables) is derived from events via materializers.

#### Events (Source of Truth)

```typescript
// packages/domain/src/events.ts
import { Events, Schema } from "@livestore/livestore"

export const events = {
  // Project events
  projectCreated: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.ProjectCreated",
    schema: Schema.Struct({
      id: Schema.String,
      name: Schema.String,
      address: Schema.optional(Schema.String),
    }),
  }),

  projectRenamed: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.ProjectRenamed",
    schema: Schema.Struct({ projectId: Schema.String, name: Schema.String }),
  }),

  // Photo events
  photoCaptured: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.PhotoCaptured",
    schema: Schema.Struct({
      id: Schema.String,
      projectId: Schema.String,
      markerId: Schema.optional(Schema.String),
      localPath: Schema.String,
      isIssue: Schema.Boolean,
      capturedAt: Schema.Date,
    }),
  }),

  photoMarkedAsIssue: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.PhotoMarkedAsIssue",
    schema: Schema.Struct({ photoId: Schema.String }),
  }),

  photoUnmarkedAsIssue: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.PhotoUnmarkedAsIssue",
    schema: Schema.Struct({ photoId: Schema.String }),
  }),

  photoLinkedToMarker: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.PhotoLinkedToMarker",
    schema: Schema.Struct({ photoId: Schema.String, markerId: Schema.String }),
  }),

  photoUploaded: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.PhotoUploaded",
    schema: Schema.Struct({ photoId: Schema.String, remotePath: Schema.String }),
  }),

  // Voice note events
  voiceNoteRecorded: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.VoiceNoteRecorded",
    schema: Schema.Struct({
      id: Schema.String,
      photoId: Schema.String,
      localPath: Schema.String,
      durationSeconds: Schema.Number,
    }),
  }),

  voiceNoteTranscribed: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.VoiceNoteTranscribed",
    schema: Schema.Struct({ voiceNoteId: Schema.String, transcription: Schema.String }),
  }),

  // Sheet/Marker events (from server sync after PDF processing)
  sheetsReceived: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.SheetsReceived",
    schema: Schema.Struct({
      projectId: Schema.String,
      sheets: Schema.Array(
        Schema.Struct({
          id: Schema.String,
          pageNumber: Schema.Number,
          sheetNumber: Schema.optional(Schema.String),
          sheetTitle: Schema.optional(Schema.String),
          discipline: Schema.optional(Schema.String),
        }),
      ),
    }),
  }),

  markersReceived: Events.synced({
    name: "v1.MarkersReceived",
    schema: Schema.Struct({
      sheetId: Schema.String,
      markers: Schema.Array(
        Schema.Struct({
          id: Schema.String,
          reference: Schema.String,
          x: Schema.Number,
          y: Schema.Number,
          targetSheetId: Schema.optional(Schema.String),
          confidence: Schema.Number,
        }),
      ),
    }),
  }),
}
```

#### State Tables (Derived from Events)

```typescript
// packages/domain/src/tables.ts
import { State, Schema } from "@livestore/livestore"

export const tables = {
  projects: State.SQLite.table({
    name: "projects",
    columns: {
      id: State.SQLite.text({ primaryKey: true }),
      name: State.SQLite.text(),
      address: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      createdAt: State.SQLite.integer({ schema: Schema.DateFromNumber }),
    },
  }),

  sheets: State.SQLite.table({
    name: "sheets",
    columns: {
      id: State.SQLite.text({ primaryKey: true }),
      projectId: State.SQLite.text(),
      pageNumber: State.SQLite.integer(),
      sheetNumber: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      sheetTitle: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      discipline: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      screenPath: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      detailPath: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
    },
  }),

  markers: State.SQLite.table({
    name: "markers",
    columns: {
      id: State.SQLite.text({ primaryKey: true }),
      sheetId: State.SQLite.text(),
      reference: State.SQLite.text(),
      x: State.SQLite.real(),
      y: State.SQLite.real(),
      targetSheetId: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      confidence: State.SQLite.real({ nullable: true }),
    },
  }),

  photos: State.SQLite.table({
    name: "photos",
    columns: {
      id: State.SQLite.text({ primaryKey: true }),
      projectId: State.SQLite.text(),
      markerId: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      localPath: State.SQLite.text(),
      remotePath: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      isIssue: State.SQLite.boolean({ default: false }),
      capturedAt: State.SQLite.integer({ schema: Schema.DateFromNumber }),
    },
  }),

  voiceNotes: State.SQLite.table({
    name: "voice_notes",
    columns: {
      id: State.SQLite.text({ primaryKey: true }),
      photoId: State.SQLite.text(),
      localPath: State.SQLite.text(),
      remotePath: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
      durationSeconds: State.SQLite.integer({ nullable: true }),
      transcription: State.SQLite.text({ nullable: true }),
    },
  }),
}
```

#### Materializers (Events â†’ State)

```typescript
// packages/domain/src/materializers.ts
import { State } from "@livestore/livestore"
import { events } from "./events"
import { tables } from "./tables"

export const materializers = State.SQLite.materializers(events, {
  projectCreated: ({ id, name, address }) =>
    tables.projects.insert({ id, name, address, createdAt: Date.now() }),

  projectRenamed: ({ projectId, name }) =>
    tables.projects.update({ name }).where({ id: projectId }),

  photoCaptured: ({ id, projectId, markerId, localPath, isIssue, capturedAt }) =>
    tables.photos.insert({
      id,
      projectId,
      markerId,
      localPath,
      isIssue,
      capturedAt: capturedAt.getTime(),
    }),

  photoMarkedAsIssue: ({ photoId }) =>
    tables.photos.update({ isIssue: true }).where({ id: photoId }),

  photoUnmarkedAsIssue: ({ photoId }) =>
    tables.photos.update({ isIssue: false }).where({ id: photoId }),

  photoLinkedToMarker: ({ photoId, markerId }) =>
    tables.photos.update({ markerId }).where({ id: photoId }),

  photoUploaded: ({ photoId, remotePath }) =>
    tables.photos.update({ remotePath }).where({ id: photoId }),

  voiceNoteRecorded: ({ id, photoId, localPath, durationSeconds }) =>
    tables.voiceNotes.insert({ id, photoId, localPath, durationSeconds }),

  voiceNoteTranscribed: ({ voiceNoteId, transcription }) =>
    tables.voiceNotes.update({ transcription }).where({ id: voiceNoteId }),

  sheetsReceived: ({ projectId, sheets }) =>
    sheets.map((sheet) => tables.sheets.insert({ ...sheet, projectId })),

  markersReceived: ({ sheetId, markers }) =>
    markers.map((marker) => tables.markers.insert({ ...marker, sheetId })),
})
```

#### Example Usage in Components

```typescript
// Reactive query - auto-updates when events change state
import { useQuery } from '@livestore/react'
import { tables } from '@sitelink/domain'

function PhotoTimeline({ markerId }: { markerId: string }) {
  const photos = useQuery(
    tables.photos
      .where({ markerId })
      .orderBy('capturedAt', 'desc')
  )

  return (
    <FlatList data={photos} renderItem={({ item }) => <PhotoCard photo={item} />} />
  )
}

// Committing events
import { useStore } from '@livestore/react'
import { events } from '@sitelink/domain'

function CaptureButton({ projectId, markerId }) {
  const { store } = useStore()

  const handleCapture = async (uri: string, isIssue: boolean) => {
    const id = crypto.randomUUID()
    const localPath = `${FileSystem.documentDirectory}photos/${id}.jpg`
    await FileSystem.copyAsync({ from: uri, to: localPath })

    store.commit(events.photoCaptured({
      id,
      projectId,
      markerId,
      localPath,
      isIssue,
      capturedAt: new Date(),
    }))
  }
}
```

### 16.3 API Endpoints (Key)

```
AUTH
POST   /api/auth/signin
POST   /api/auth/signout
GET    /api/auth/session
POST   /api/auth/checkout/:slug
GET    /api/auth/portal

PROJECTS
GET    /api/projects
POST   /api/projects
GET    /api/projects/:id
PATCH  /api/projects/:id
DELETE /api/projects/:id

PLANS
POST   /api/projects/:id/plans          (upload)
GET    /api/projects/:id/sheets
GET    /api/sheets/:id
GET    /api/sheets/:id/markers
GET    /api/sheets/:id/search?q=

PHOTOS
GET    /api/projects/:id/photos
GET    /api/markers/:id/photos
POST   /api/photos                       (upload)
PATCH  /api/photos/:id

VOICE NOTES
POST   /api/photos/:id/voice            (upload)
GET    /api/voice-notes/:id/transcription

AI
POST   /api/projects/:id/summary        (generate daily)
POST   /api/photos/:id/rfi              (generate RFI draft)

SHARE
POST   /api/projects/:id/share-link
POST   /api/summaries/:id/share-link
GET    /api/share/:token                (public)
```

```
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

#### How LiveStore Sync Works

1. **User captures photo** â†’ Event committed to local LiveStore
2. **Event persisted** â†’ Stored in local SQLite eventlog
3. **Materializer runs** â†’ State (photos table) updated
4. **Reactive query fires** â†’ UI updates immediately
5. **When online** â†’ Events pushed to sync backend via WebSocket
6. **Photo file uploaded** â†’ Separate upload to R2, then `photoUploaded` event

#### Event Sourcing Benefits for Construction

| Scenario                       | Traditional CRUD                         | LiveStore Event Sourcing                 |
| ------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| "When was this issue flagged?" | Need separate audit log                  | `photoMarkedAsIssue` event has timestamp |
| "Who marked it?"               | Track `updatedBy` field                  | Event has actor built-in                 |
| "Undo issue flag"              | `UPDATE isIssue = false` (loses history) | Emit `photoUnmarkedAsIssue` event        |
| "Project state from last week" | Need point-in-time backup                | Replay events up to that date            |

```
---

## 17. Pricing Strategy

### 17.1 Rationale

**Why flat pricing (not per-user):**
- Small contractors have thin margins
- Per-user pricing creates friction for team adoption
- Competitors' per-user model gets expensive fast
- Flat pricing is simpler to understand and budget

**Why no free tier:**
- Free users have support burden without revenue
- Encourages trial â†’ conversion flow
- View-only sharing serves the "free" use case
- Avoids competing with Fieldwire's free tier directly

**Price point justification:**
- Starter ($29): Cheaper than 1 Fieldwire Pro seat ($39)
- Pro ($79): Cheaper than 2 Fieldwire Pro seats ($78)
- Business ($149): Cheaper than 4 Fieldwire Pro seats ($156)

### 17.2 Competitor Pricing Comparison

| Product | 1 User | 5 Users | 15 Users |
|---------|--------|---------|----------|
| Fieldwire Pro | $39/mo | $195/mo | $585/mo |
| Autodesk Build | $135/mo | $675/mo | $2,025/mo |
| Procore | ~$375/mo | ~$375/mo | ~$500/mo |
| **SiteLink Pro** | **$79/mo** | **$79/mo** | **$79/mo** |

### 17.3 Upgrade Prompts

**Soft prompts (non-blocking):**
- Trial ending banner (day 12, day 13, day 14)
- "Upgrade for AI features" tooltip on locked features
- Monthly usage report with upgrade CTA

**Hard prompts (blocking):**
- Trial expired: Can view but not add content
- Project limit hit: Must upgrade or archive project
- Sheet limit hit: Must upgrade to upload more

---

## 18. MVP Scope & Phasing

### 18.1 Phase 1: Core MVP (Weeks 1-4)

**Foundation (Week 1):**
- [ ] LiveStore + Expo integration (@livestore/adapter-expo)
- [ ] LiveStore sync backend on Cloudflare (@livestore/sync-cf)
- [ ] Domain package with events, tables, materializers
- [ ] Biometric offline auth (SecureStore + expo-local-authentication)

**Core Features (Weeks 2-4):**
- [ ] OAuth sign-in (Google, Microsoft)
- [ ] Project creation
- [ ] Plan upload + processing pipeline
- [ ] Sheet viewer with callout markers
- [ ] Callout navigation (sheet-to-sheet linking)
- [ ] Camera with callout linking
- [ ] Issue toggle on camera
- [ ] Photo timeline per callout
- [ ] Voice note recording (audio only, no transcription)
- [ ] Basic project sharing (view-only link)
- [ ] Offline sheet viewing (automatic via LiveStore)
- [ ] Polar payment integration
- [ ] Basic subscription management

**Out of scope for Phase 1:**
- Voice transcription
- Plan text search
- Daily summary generation
- RFI generation
- Team member management (beyond owner)
- Notification system
- Feature request system

### 18.2 Phase 2: AI Features (Weeks 5-8)

- [ ] Voice note transcription (Whisper)
- [ ] Plan text search (full-text index)
- [ ] Photo text extraction (OCR on photos)
- [ ] Daily summary generation (LLM)
- [ ] Share daily report (hosted page + PDF)

### 18.3 Phase 3: Polish & Growth (Weeks 9-12)

- [ ] Team member invitation
- [ ] Role-based permissions
- [ ] Notification system (push)
- [ ] RFI draft generation
- [ ] Feature request screen
- [ ] Analytics integration (PostHog)
- [ ] Performance optimization
- [ ] LiveStore devtools integration (debugging)

### 18.4 Success Metrics for MVP

| Metric | Target | Measurement |
|--------|--------|-------------|
| Signup to first upload | >50% | Analytics |
| Day 7 retention | >30% | Analytics |
| Photos per active user per day | >3 | Analytics |
| Trial-to-paid conversion | >10% | Polar |
| NPS | >40 | In-app survey |
| Support tickets per user | <0.5/month | Support system |

## Appendix A: Items Added Beyond User's Initial Request

The following items were added to ensure completeness:

1. **User Personas (Section 3)** - Detailed personas to guide UX decisions
2. **Design System (Section 15)** - Colors, typography, spacing, components for UI consistency
3. **Data Models (Section 16.2)** - LiveStore events, tables, and materializers for event sourcing
4. **API Endpoints (Section 16.3)** - Key API routes
5. **Offline Architecture (Section 16.4)** - LiveStore-based offline-first architecture with automatic sync
6. **Success Metrics (Section 18.4)** - How to measure MVP success
7. **Discipline badges** - Color-coded sheet categorization (ARCH, ELEC, etc.)
8. **Demo project** - Pre-loaded sample for new users to explore
9. **Photo text extraction** - OCR on captured photos (not just plans)
10. **Sheet filters** - Filter by discipline in sheet list
11. **Quick feedback prompt** - In-app feedback after 10 photos
12. **Error states** - Handling for upload failures, sync failures
13. **Deep links** - Notification â†’ specific screen navigation
```
